<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Item&nbsp;2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Item&nbsp;7.01 Regulation&nbsp;FD Disclosure.</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On September&nbsp;27, 2004, NACCO Industries, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;)
will post on its website at www.nacco.com, additional historical
quarterly financial data and update the schedules that were previously
posted to the website on August&nbsp;13, 2004. A copy of the additional
data is attached as Exhibit&nbsp;99 to this Current Report on Form 8-K.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Current Report on Form 8-K and the information attached
hereto are being furnished by the Company pursuant to Item&nbsp;2.02 and
7.01 of Form 8-K, insofar as they disclose historical information
regarding the Company&#146;s results of operations.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In accordance with General Instruction B.2 and B.6 of Form 8-K,
the information in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit
99, shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for the purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the
Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to
the liability of that section, nor shall it be deemed incorporated by
reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended,
except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a
filing.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Item&nbsp;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits.</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As described in Item&nbsp;2.02 and 7.01 of this Current Report on Form
8-K, the following Exhibit is furnished as part of this Current Report
on Form 8-K.

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(1)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Net working capital is equal to accounts receivable, net plus inventories less accounts payable.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(2)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Cash flow before financing activities is equal to net cash provided by (used for) operating activities plus net cash provided by (used for) investing activities.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(3)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Return on equity is equal to the sum of the previous 4 quarters net income divided by average equity calculated over the last 5 quarters.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(4)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Total debt presented excludes the obligations of the project mining subsidiaries. The project mining subsidiaries&#146; utility customers arrange and
guarantee the financing of the project mining subsidiaries. These obligations are without recourse to and are not guaranteed by North American Coal
or NACCO.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(1)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Net working capital is equal to accounts receivable, net plus inventories less accounts payable.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(2)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Cash flow before financing activities is equal to net cash provided by (used for) operating activities plus net cash provided by (used for) investing activities.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(3)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Return on equity is equal to the sum of the previous 4 quarters net income divided by average equity calculated over the last 5 quarters.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(1)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Net working capital is equal to accounts receivable, net plus inventories less accounts payable.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(2)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Cash flow before financing activities is equal to net cash provided by (used for) operating activities plus net cash provided by (used for) investing activities.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(3)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Return on equity is equal to the sum of the previous 4 quarters net income divided by average equity calculated over the last 5 quarters.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(1)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Net working capital is equal to accounts receivable, net plus inventories less accounts payable.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(2)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Cash flow before financing activities is equal to net cash provided by (used for) operating activities plus net cash provided by (used for) investing activities.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(3)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Return on equity is equal to the sum of the previous 4 quarters net income divided by average equity calculated over the last 5 quarters.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(1)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Net working capital is equal to accounts receivable, net plus inventories less accounts payable.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(2)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Cash flow before financing activities is equal to net cash provided by (used for) operating activities plus net cash provided by (used for) investing activities.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(3)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Return on equity is equal to the sum of the previous 4 quarters net income divided by average equity calculated over the last 5 quarters.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">11 of 12


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(1)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Cash flow before financing activities is equal to net cash provided by (used for) operating activities plus net cash provided by (used for) investing activities.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right"><B>(2)</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Return on equity is equal to the sum of the previous 4 quarters net income divided by average equity calculated over the last 5 quarters.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
